Usage:

  --help
       Show available options
  --list
       List the available time stepper kernels and their number.
       Description of the time steppers is available at wrappers.h
  --verify <bool>
       Verify the correctness of the selected time stepper using
       the provided domain and topology information
       (This option disables performance measurement experiments)

General experiment parameters:
  --target-ts <integer>
       Select the desired time stepper kernel
       (can acquire the available time stepper through --list option)
  --target-kernel <integer>
       Select the desired stencil kernel
       (can acquire the available kernels through --list option)
  --nx <integer>
       Global domain size in the x direction
  --ny <integer>
       Global domain size in the y direction
  --nz <integer>
       Global domain size in the z direction
  --nt <integer>
       The desired number of time steps
  --npx <integer>
       Number of MPI processes across the x direction
  --npy <integer>
       Number of MPI processes across the y direction
  --npz <integer>
       Number of MPI processes across the z direction
  --n-tests <integer>
       Specify how many times the time stepper is run at the
       performance measurement experiments
  --alignment <integer>
       Specify the memory alignment value (in bytes) of the
       allocated domain arrays
  --disable-source-point
       disables the source point update in the solution domain

Display options:
  --verbose <bool>
       Show the used configuration information
  --debug <bool>
       Print detailed debugging information

Specialized arguments:
  --t-dim <integer>    (specific to the Diamond methods)
       Specifies the value of unrolling in time
  --z-mpi-contig <bool>    (Specific to standard methods: 0-1)
       Uses contiguous MPI datatype in the z direction of the MPI
       topology at the standard methods
  --halo-concatenate <integer>  (experimental feature)
       Explicitly concatenate halo information before send and unpack them
       at receiving end using multi-threading.
       (Works for decomposition across X and Y only)
  --thread-group-size <integer>   (specific to diamond tiling)
       Set the thread group size for methods supporting multiple thread groups
  --thx <integer>    (specific to diamond tiling)
       Set threads number along the x-axis
  --thy <integer>    (specific to diamond tiling)
       Set threads number along the y-axis in the diamond tile
  --thz <integer>    (specific to diamond tiling)
       Set threads number along the z-axis
  --thc <integer>    (specific to diamond tiling solar kernels)
       Set threads number per component
  --cache-size <integer>
       The usable last level cache size for spatial blocking
  --wavefront <bool>
       Indicate whether to use wavefront in the tile. 1 for yes and 0 for no (default 1)
  --num-wavefronts <int>
       Set the number of wavefronts updated per wavefront iteration (default 1)
  --mwd-type <int>
       Select one of the MWD implementations from the one available at --list option
  --use-omp-stat-sched
       Use OpenMP static schedule instead of static,1 at the spatial blocking time steppers
  --threads threads[:block[:stride]]    (specific to diamond tiling)
       Set the threads number, blocks, and strides when using internal affinitiy control
